Source Code

These source-code files were obtained by digitally photographing an Artemis 72 program listing from a private collection and then modifying pre-existing Comanche 55 (Apollo 11) source files to incorporate changes. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images may be available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 072 OF AGC PROGRAM ARTEMIS 
	BY NASA 2021114-011 11:40 FEB. 26, 1971

	THIS AGC PROGRAM SHALL ALSO BE REFERRED TO AS
				COLOSSUS 3
	THIS PROGRAM IS INTENDED FOR USE IN THE CM AS SPECIFIED
	IN REPORT R-577.  THIS PROGRAM WAS PREPARED UNDER OSR
	PROJECT 55-23890, SPONSORED BY THE MANNED SPACECRAFT
	CENTER OF THE NATIONAL AERONAUTICS AND SPACE
	ADMINISTRATION THROUGH CONTRACT NAS 9-4065 WITH THE
	CHARLES STARK DRAPER LABORATORY, MASSACHUSETTS INSTITUTE OF
	TECHNOLOGY, CAMBRIDGE, MASS.

001547,000005:                                                                                                 #                 build 072.  This is for the Command Module's (CM) 
001548,000006:                                                                                                 #                 Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), we believe for 
001549,000007:                                                                                                 #                 Apollo 15-17.

Page 38 

001566,000024:                                                                                                 #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001567,000025: 
001568,000026:                                                                                                 #         EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001569,000027:                                                                                                 #                 OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001570,000028:                                                                                                 #                 CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE:
001571,000029: 
001572,000030:                                                                                                 #                                         X       EQUALS  START
001573,000031:                                                                                                 #                                         Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001574,000032:                                                                                                 #                                         Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001575,000033: 
001576,000034:                                                                                                 #                 (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001577,000035:                                                                                                 #                 (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001578,000036:                                                                                                 #                  USUALLY NUMERIC,  IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D, ETC.              )
001579,000037: 
001580,000038: 
001581,000039:                                                                                                 #         EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001582,000040:                                                                                                 #                 AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE:
001583,000041: 
001584,000042:                                                                                                 #                                         X       EQUALS  Y
001585,000043: 
001586,000044: 
001587,000045:                                                                                                 #         = MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001588,000046:                                                                                                 #                 (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001589,000047: 
001590,000048:                                                                                                 #                                         X       =       Y
001591,000049: 
001592,000050: 
001593,000051:                                                                                                 #         THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001594,000052:                                                                                                 #         THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001595,000053: 
001596,000054:                                                                                                 #                 M REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001597,000055:                                                                                                 #                      B   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001598,000056:                                                                                                 #                          INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001599,000057:                                                                                                 #                      I   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001600,000058:                                                                                                 #                          INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001601,000059:                                                                                                 #                          INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001602,000060: 
001603,000061:                                                                                                 #                 SIZE IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001604,000062: 
001605,000063:                                                                                                 #                 N INDICATES THE NATURE OF PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001606,000064:                                                                                                 #                      PL MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001607,000065:                                                                                                 #                      DSP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001608,000066:                                                                                                 #                      PRM MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001609,000067:                                                                                                 #                          IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001610,000068:                                                                                                 #                          PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001611,000069:                                                                                                 #                      TMP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001612,000070:                                                                                                 #                          IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001613,000071:                                                                                                 #                          IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001614,000072:                                                                                                 #                          PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001615,000073:                                                                                                 #                          CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 39 

001617,000075:                                                                                                 #                          IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001618,000076:                                                                                                 #                          IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001619,000077:                                                                                                 #                      IN  MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001620,000078:                                                                                                 #                          TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001621,000079:                                                                                                 #                      OUT MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001622,000080:                                                                                                 #                          TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001623,000081:

Page 40 

001625,000083: 
001626,000084:                                                                                                 #         SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001627,000085: 
001628,000086: ???????                        A                 EQUALS   0                                     
001629,000087: ???????                        L                 EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001630,000088: ???????                        Q                 EQUALS   2                                     
001631,000089: ???????                        EBANK             EQUALS   3                                     
001632,000090: ???????                        FBANK             EQUALS   4                                     
001633,000091: ???????                        Z                 EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001634,000092: ???????                        BBANK             EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF)
001635,000093:                                                                                                 #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001636,000094: 
001637,000095: ???????                        ARUPT             EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001638,000096: ???????                        LRUPT             EQUALS   11                                    
001639,000097: ???????                        QRUPT             EQUALS   12                                    
001640,000098: ???????                        SAMPTIME          EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001641,000099: ???????                        ZRUPT             EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001642,000100: ???????                        BANKRUPT          EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK
001643,000101: ???????                        BRUPT             EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001644,000102: 
001645,000103: ???????                        CYR               EQUALS   20                                    
001646,000104: ???????                        SR                EQUALS   21                                    
001647,000105: ???????                        CYL               EQUALS   22                                    
001648,000106: ???????                        EDOP              EQUALS   23                                    #  EDITS INTERPRETIVE OPERATION CODE PAIRS.
001649,000107: 
001650,000108: 
001651,000109: ???????                        TIME2             EQUALS   24                                    
001652,000110: ???????                        TIME1             EQUALS   25                                    
001653,000111: ???????                        TIME3             EQUALS   26                                    
001654,000112: ???????                        TIME4             EQUALS   27                                    
001655,000113: ???????                        TIME5             EQUALS   30                                    
001656,000114: ???????                        TIME6             EQUALS   31                                    
001657,000115: ???????                        CDUX              EQUALS   32                                    
001658,000116: ???????                        CDUY              EQUALS   33                                    
001659,000117: ???????                        CDUZ              EQUALS   34                                    
001660,000118: ???????                        CDUT              EQUALS   35                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION CDU (WAS OPTY)
001661,000119: ???????                        CDUS              EQUALS   36                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT CDU (WAS OPTX)
001662,000120: ???????                        PIPAX             EQUALS   37                                    
001663,000121: ???????                        PIPAY             EQUALS   40                                    
001664,000122: ???????                        PIPAZ             EQUALS   41                                    
001665,000123: ???????                        BMAGX             EQUALS   42                                    
001666,000124: ???????                        BMAGY             EQUALS   43                                    
001667,000125: ???????                        BMAGZ             EQUALS   44                                    
001668,000126: ???????                        INLINK            EQUALS   45                                    
001669,000127: ???????                        RNRAD             EQUALS   46                                    
001670,000128: ???????                        GYROCMD           EQUALS   47                                    
001671,000129: ???????                        CDUXCMD           EQUALS   50                                    
001672,000130: ???????                        CDUYCMD           EQUALS   51                                    
001673,000131: ???????                        CDUZCMD           EQUALS   52                                    
001674,000132: ???????                        CDUTCMD           EQUALS   53                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION COMMAND (WAS OPTYCMD).
001675,000133: ???????  0000053               TVCYAW            EQUALS   CDUTCMD                               #  SPS YAW COMMAND IN TVC MODE.
001676,000134:

Page 41 

001678,000136: ???????                        CDUSCMD           EQUALS   54                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT COMMAND (WAS OPTXCMD).
001679,000137: ???????  0000054               TVCPITCH          EQUALS   CDUSCMD                               #  SPS PITCH COMMAND IN TVC MODE.
001680,000138:                                                                                                 #  REGISTERS 55-60 ARE COUNTERS WHICH ARE NOT PRESENTLY WIRED, AND SO MAY BE USED WITH CARE
001681,000139:

001688,000146: ???????                        X2                EQUALS   39D                                   #  TO THE WORK AREA
